06778 
06779 WCHAR ff_convert (  /* Converted code, 0 means conversion error */
06780     WCHAR   src,    /* Character code to be converted */
06781     UINT    dir     /* 0: Unicode to OEMCP, 1: OEMCP to Unicode */
06782 )
06783 {
06784     const WCHAR *p;
06785     WCHAR c;
06786     int i, n, li, hi;
06787 
06788 
06789     if (src < 0x80) {   /* ASCII */
06790         c = src;
06791     } else {
06792         if (dir) {      /* OEMCP to unicode */
06793             p = oem2uni;
06794             hi = sizeof(oem2uni) / 4 - 1;
06795         } else {        /* Unicode to OEMCP */
06796             p = uni2oem;
06797             hi = sizeof(uni2oem) / 4 - 1;
06798         }
06799         li = 0;
06800         for (n = 16; n; n--) {
06801             i = li + (hi - li) / 2;
06802             if (src == p[i * 2]) break;
06803             if (src > p[i * 2])
06804                 li = i;
06805             else
06806                 hi = i;
06807         }
06808         c = n ? p[i * 2 + 1] : 0;
06809     }
06810 
06811     return c;
06812 }
